 is saal makar sakranti 15 janvari ke din puure deshbhar main manaai jaaegi
 Usually this festival is celebrated on 14 January but this time it is falling on 15 January
 makar sankranti surya upasna kaa vishesh parv he
 From this day onwards, the sun starts to Uttarayan and from then onwards, the cold of winter starts decreasing in the northern hemisphere of the earth
 manyata he ki makar sankranti ke din surya dhanu raashi ko chhod makar raashi main pravesh karata he
 For this reason, this solstice is known as Makar Sankranti
 makar sankranti par surya aradhana ke saath apane isht dev kii aradhana bhi shubh mana jaati he
